5.	Ano mufaro munhu uyo anoita mutsa, acharuramiswa mhaka pakutongwa.
6.	Akarurama haakanganikwi, acharamba achirangarirwa nokusingaperi.
7.	Haangatyi mashoko ezvinhu zvakaipa, moyo wake wakasimba uchavimba.
waMwari.

achaparara.
